1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`

4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`


Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching

# Add Evaluation Metadata Field to Flipt (Proto + Go)

**Repository:** github.com/sg-evals/flipt--3d5a345f (mirror of github.com/sg-evals)/flipt--3d5a345f (mirror of flipt-io/flipt)
**Access Scope:** You may modify files in `rpc/flipt/evaluation/` (protobuf schema + generated code) and `internal/server/evaluation/` (Go server). You may read any other files to understand existing patterns.

## Context

Flipt is a feature flag platform built with Go and gRPC. Its API is defined in Protocol Buffer (`.proto`) files, with generated Go code alongside. The evaluation server constructs protobuf response objects returned to clients.

Operators have requested that evaluation responses include a `segment_match_type` field so clients can see whether the evaluation matched a segment using `ALL` (all constraints matched) or `ANY` (at least one constraint matched) logic. This information is already available in the evaluation flow but is not exposed in the response.

## Task

Add a `segment_match_type` string field to the evaluation responses. This requires changes to **both** the protobuf schema (`.proto` file) and the Go server code that constructs responses — a cross-language change.

**YOU MUST IMPLEMENT CODE CHANGES.**

### Requirements

1. **Protobuf schema change** — Add `string segment_match_type` to the `VariantEvaluationResponse` message in the evaluation proto file. Determine the next sequential tag by examining existing fields in the message. The value should be "ALL", "ANY", or "" (empty when no segment matched).

2. **Generated Go code change** — Add the corresponding `SegmentMatchType string` field and getter method to the Go generated code (`.pb.go` file). Match the exact patterns used by existing fields. Do NOT regenerate code with protoc — manually add the field.

3. **Server code change** — In the evaluation server, populate `SegmentMatchType` on the response after evaluation logic determines which rule matched. The evaluation must set this field for variant evaluations, and batch responses should include it too.

4. **Determine the source value** — The storage layer carries segment operator information on evaluation rules that indicates ALL vs ANY. Find this type and trace how the operator maps to the string values you need.

## Success Criteria

- Evaluation proto has `segment_match_type` field in `VariantEvaluationResponse`
- Generated Go code has matching `SegmentMatchType` field and getter
- Server code populates `SegmentMatchType` from the rule's segment operator
- Proto tag number is valid (no collision with existing fields)
- Changes span both proto and Go files (cross-language change)
- Go code compiles: `go build ./internal/server/evaluation/...`

   - Assigned to response at correct points (lines 256, 282)

   - Updated all return statements to include the new field

for a multi-variate flag and entity.\nfunc (s *Server) Variant(ctx context.Context, r *rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.VariantEvaluationResponse, error) {\n\tenv, err := s.store.Get(ctx, r.EnvironmentKey)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\t// try to get the environment from the context\n\t\t// this is for backwards compatibility with v1\n\t\tenv, err = s.store.GetFromContext(ctx)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tstore, err := env.EvaluationStore()\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tflag, err := store.GetFlag(ctx, storage.NewResource(r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey, storage.WithReference(r.Reference)))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tif flag.Type != core.FlagType_VARIANT_FLAG_TYPE {\n\t\treturn nil, errs.ErrInvalidf(\"flag type %s invalid\", flag.Type)\n\t}\n\n\tresp, err := s.variant(ctx, store, env, flag, r)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tif s.tracingEnabled {\n\t\ts.addEvaluationEvent(ctx, env, r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey, r.EntityId, r.RequestId,\n\t\t\ttracing.AttributeMatch.Bool(resp.Match),\n\t\t\ttracing.AttributeVariant.String(resp.VariantKey),\n\t\t\ttracing.AttributeReason.String(tracing.ReasonToValue(resp.Reason)),\n\t\t\ttracing.AttributeSegments.StringSlice(resp.SegmentKeys),\n\t\t\ttracing.AttributeFlagTypeVariant,\n\t\t)\n\t}\n\n\treturn resp, nil\n}\n\nfunc (s *Server) variant(ctx context.Context, store storage.ReadOnlyStore, env environments.Environment, flag *core.Flag, r *rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.VariantEvaluationResponse, error) {\n\tvar (\n\t\tresp = &rpcevaluation.VariantEvaluationResponse{\n\t\t\tFlagKey:   flag.Key,\n\t\t\tRequestId: r.RequestId,\n\t\t}\n\t\terr      error\n\t\tlastRank int32\n\n\t\tstartTime       = time.Now().UTC()\n\t\tenvironmentAttr = metrics.AttributeEnvironment.String(env.Key())\n\t\tnamespaceAttr   = metrics.AttributeNamespace.String(r.NamespaceKey)\n\t\tflagAttr        = metrics.AttributeFlag.String(r.FlagKey)\n\t)\n\n\tmetrics.EvaluationsTotal.Add(ctx, 1, metric.WithAttributeSet(attribute.NewSet(environmentAttr, namespaceAttr, flagAttr)))\n\n\tdefer func() {\n\t\tif err == nil {\n\t\t\tmetrics.EvaluationResultsTotal.Add(ctx, 1,\n\t\t\t\tmetric.WithAttributeSet(\n\t\t\t\t\tattribute.NewSet(\n\t\t\t\t\t\tenvironmentAttr,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tnamespaceAttr,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tflagAttr,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tmetrics.AttributeMatch.Bool(resp.Match),\n\t\t\t\t\t\tmetrics.AttributeSegments.StringSlice(resp.SegmentKeys),\n\t\t\t\t\t\tmetrics.AttributeReason.String(resp.Reason.String()),\n\t\t\t\t\t\tmetrics.AttributeValue.String(resp.VariantKey),\n\t\t\t\t\t\tmetrics.AttributeFlagType.String(\"variant\"),\n\t\t\t\t\t),\n\t\t\t\t),\n\t\t\t)\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tmetrics.EvaluationErrorsTotal.Add(ctx, 1, metric.WithAttributeSet(attribute.NewSet(environmentAttr, namespaceAttr, flagAttr)))\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tmetrics.EvaluationLatency.Record(\n\t\t\tctx,\n\t\t\tfloat64(time.Since(startTime).Nanoseconds())/1e6,\n\t\t\tmetric.WithAttributeSet(\n\t\t\t\tattribute.NewSet(\n\t\t\t\t\tenvironmentAttr,\n\t\t\t\t\tnamespaceAttr,\n\t\t\t\t\tflagAttr,\n\t\t\t\t),\n\t\t\t),\n\t\t)\n\t}()\n\n\tif flag.DefaultVariant != nil {\n\t\tdv, ok := getVariant(flag.GetDefaultVariant(), flag.Variants...)\n\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"default variant not found: %q\", flag.GetDefaultVariant())\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tvar attachment string\n\t\tif dv.Attachment != nil {\n\t\t\ta, err := dv.Attachment.MarshalJSON()\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tattachment = string(a)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tresp.Reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_DEFAULT_EVALUATION_REASON\n\t\tresp.VariantKey = dv.Key\n\t\tresp.VariantAttachment = attachment\n\t}\n\n\tif !flag.Enabled {\n\t\tresp.Match = false\n\t\tresp.Reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_FLAG_DISABLED_EVALUATION_REASON\n\t\treturn resp, nil\n\t}\n\n\trules, err := store.GetEvaluationRules(ctx, storage.NewResource(r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tif len(rules) == 0 {\n\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"no rules match\")\n\t\treturn resp, nil\n\t}\n\n\tvar segmentMatchType string\n\n\t// rule loop\n\tfor _, rule := range rules {\n\t\tif rule.Rank < lastRank {\n\t\t\treturn nil, errs.ErrInvalidf(\"rule rank: %d detected out of order\", rule.Rank)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tlastRank = rule.Rank\n\n\t\tsegmentKeys := make([]string, 0, len(rule.Segments))\n\t\tsegmentMatches := 0\n\n\t\tfor k, v := range rule.Segments {\n\t\t\tmatched, reason, err := s.matchConstraints(r.Context, v.Constraints, v.MatchType, r.EntityId)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif matched {\n\t\t\t\ts.logger.Debug(reason)\n\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys = append(segmentKeys, k)\n\t\t\t\tsegmentMatches++\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tswitch rule.SegmentOperator {\n\t\tcase core.SegmentOperator_OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR:\n\t\t\tif segmentMatches < 1 {\n\t\t\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"did not match ANY segments\")\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tsegmentMatchType = \"ANY\"\n\t\tcase core.SegmentOperator_AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR:\n\t\t\tif len(rule.Segments) != segmentMatches {\n\t\t\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"did not match ALL segments\")\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tsegmentMatchType = \"ALL\"\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif len(segmentKeys) > 0 {\n\t\t\tresp.SegmentKeys = segmentKeys\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tdistributions, err := store.GetEvaluationDistributions(ctx, storage.NewResource(r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey), storage.NewID(rule.ID))\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tvar (\n\t\t\tvalidDistributions []*storage.EvaluationDistribution\n\t\t\tbuckets            []int\n\t\t)\n\n\t\tfor _, d := range distributions {\n\t\t\t// don't include 0% rollouts\n\t\t\tif d.Rollout > 0 {\n\t\t\t\tvalidDistributions = append(validDistributions, d)\n\n\t\t\t\tif buckets == nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tbucket := int(d.Rollout * percentMultiplier)\n\t\t\t\t\tbuckets = append(buckets, bucket)\n\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\tbucket := buckets[len(buckets)-1] + int(d.Rollout*percentMultiplier)\n\t\t\t\t\tbuckets = append(buckets, bucket)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// no distributions for rule\n\t\t// match is true here because it did match the segment/rule\n\t\tif len(validDistributions) == 0 {\n\t\t\ts.logger.Info(\"no distributions for rule\")\n\t\t\tresp.Match = true\n\t\t\tresp.Reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON\n\t\t\tresp.SegmentMatchType = segmentMatchType\n\t\t\treturn resp, nil\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tvar (\n\t\t\tbucket = crc32Num(r.EntityId, r.FlagKey)\n\t\t\t// sort.SearchInts searches for x in a sorted slice of ints and returns the index\n\t\t\t// as specified by Search. The return value is the index to insert x if x is\n\t\t\t// not present (it could be len(a)).\n\t\t\tindex = sort.SearchInts(buckets, int(bucket)+1)\n\t\t)\n\n\t\t// if index is outside of our existing buckets then it does not match any distribution\n\t\tif index == len(validDistributions) {\n\t\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"did not match any distributions\")\n\t\t\tresp.Match = false\n\t\t\treturn resp, nil\n\t\t}\n\n\t\td := validDistributions[index]\n\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"matched distribution\", zap.Reflect(\"evaluation_distribution\", d))\n\n\t\tresp.Match = true\n\t\tresp.VariantKey = d.VariantKey\n\t\tresp.VariantAttachment = d.VariantAttachment\n\t\tresp.Reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON\n\t\tresp.SegmentMatchType = segmentMatchType\n\t\treturn resp, nil\n\t} // end rule loop\n\n\treturn resp, nil\n}\n\n// Boolean evaluates a request for a boolean flag and entity.\nfunc (s *Server) Boolean(ctx context.Context, r *rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.BooleanEvaluationResponse, error) {\n\tenv, err := s.store.Get(ctx, r.EnvironmentKey)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\t// try to get the environment from the context\n\t\t// this is for backwards compatibility with v1\n\t\tenv, err = s.store.GetFromContext(ctx)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tstore, err := env.EvaluationStore()\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tflag, err := store.GetFlag(ctx, storage.NewResource(r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey, storage.WithReference(r.Reference)))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tif flag.Type != core.FlagType_BOOLEAN_FLAG_TYPE {\n\t\treturn nil, errs.ErrInvalidf(\"flag type %s invalid\", flag.Type)\n\t}\n\n\tresp, err := s.boolean(ctx, store, env, flag, r)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tif s.tracingEnabled {\n\t\ts.addEvaluationEvent(ctx, env, r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey, r.EntityId, r.RequestId,\n\t\t\ttracing.AttributeVariant.Bool(resp.Enabled),\n\t\t\ttracing.AttributeReason.String(tracing.ReasonToValue(resp.Reason)),\n\t\t\ttracing.AttributeSegments.StringSlice(resp.SegmentKeys),\n\t\t\ttracing.AttributeFlagTypeBoolean,\n\t\t)\n\t}\n\n\treturn resp, nil\n}\n\nfunc (s *Server) boolean(ctx context.Context, store storage.ReadOnlyStore, env environments.Environment, flag *core.Flag, r *rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.BooleanEvaluationResponse, error) {\n\trollouts, err := store.GetEvaluationRollouts(ctx, storage.NewResource(r.NamespaceKey, flag.Key, storage.WithReference(r.Reference)))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tvar (\n\t\tresp = &rpcevaluation.BooleanEvaluationResponse{\n\t\t\tRequestId: r.RequestId,\n\t\t}\n\t\tlastRank int32\n\t)\n\n\tvar (\n\t\tstartTime       = time.Now().UTC()\n\t\tenvironmentAttr = metrics.AttributeEnvironment.String(env.Key())\n\t\tnamespaceAttr   = metrics.AttributeNamespace.String(r.NamespaceKey)\n\t\tflagAttr        = metrics.AttributeFlag.String(r.FlagKey)\n\t)\n\n\tmetrics.EvaluationsTotal.Add(ctx, 1, metric.WithAttributeSet(attribute.NewSet(environmentAttr, namespaceAttr, flagAttr)))\n\n\tdefer func() {\n\t\tif err == nil {\n\t\t\tmetrics.EvaluationResultsTotal.Add(ctx, 1,\n\t\t\t\tmetric.WithAttributeSet(\n\t\t\t\t\tattribute.NewSet(\n\t\t\t\t\t\tenvironmentAttr,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tnamespaceAttr,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tflagAttr,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tmetrics.AttributeValue.Bool(resp.Enabled),\n\t\t\t\t\t\tmetrics.AttributeReason.String(resp.Reason.String()),\n\t\t\t\t\t\tmetrics.AttributeFlagType.String(\"boolean\"),\n\t\t\t\t\t\tmetrics.AttributeSegments.StringSlice(resp.SegmentKeys),\n\t\t\t\t\t),\n\t\t\t\t),\n\t\t\t)\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tmetrics.EvaluationErrorsTotal.Add(ctx, 1, metric.WithAttributeSet(attribute.NewSet(environmentAttr, namespaceAttr, flagAttr)))\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tmetrics.EvaluationLatency.Record(\n\t\t\tctx,\n\t\t\tfloat64(time.Since(startTime).Nanoseconds())/1e6,\n\t\t\tmetric.WithAttributeSet(\n\t\t\t\tattribute.NewSet(\n\t\t\t\t\tenvironmentAttr,\n\t\t\t\t\tnamespaceAttr,\n\t\t\t\t\tflagAttr,\n\t\t\t\t),\n\t\t\t),\n\t\t)\n\t}()\n\n\tfor _, rollout := range rollouts {\n\t\tif rollout.Rank < lastRank {\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"rollout rank: %d detected out of order\", rollout.Rank)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tlastRank = rollout.Rank\n\n\t\tif rollout.Threshold != nil {\n\t\t\t// consistent hashing based on the entity id and flag key.\n\t\t\thash := crc32.ChecksumIEEE([]byte(r.EntityId + r.FlagKey))\n\n\t\t\tnormalizedValue := float32(int(hash) % 100)\n\n\t\t\t// if this case does not hold, fall through to the next rollout.\n\t\t\tif normalizedValue < rollout.Threshold.Percentage {\n\t\t\t\tresp.Enabled = rollout.Threshold.Value\n\t\t\t\tresp.Reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON\n\t\t\t\tresp.FlagKey = flag.Key\n\t\t\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"threshold based matched\", zap.Int(\"rank\", int(rollout.Rank)), zap.String(\"rollout_type\", \"threshold\"))\n\t\t\t\treturn resp, nil\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t} else if rollout.Segment != nil {\n\n\t\t\tvar (\n\t\t\t\tsegmentMatches = 0\n\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys    = []string{}\n\t\t\t)\n\n\t\t\tfor k, v := range rollout.Segment.Segments {\n\t\t\t\tmatched, reason, err := s.matchConstraints(r.Context, v.Constraints, v.MatchType, r.EntityId)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\t// if we don't match the segment, fall through to the next rollout.\n\t\t\t\tif matched {\n\t\t\t\t\ts.logger.Debug(reason)\n\t\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys = append(segmentKeys, k)\n\t\t\t\t\tsegmentMatches++\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tswitch rollout.Segment.SegmentOperator {\n\t\t\tcase core.SegmentOperator_OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR:\n\t\t\t\tif segmentMatches < 1 {\n\t\t\t\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"did not match ANY segments\")\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tcase core.SegmentOperator_AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR:\n\t\t\t\tif len(rollout.Segment.Segments) != segmentMatches {\n\t\t\t\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"did not match ALL segments\")\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tresp.Enabled = rollout.Segment.Value\n\t\t\tresp.Reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON\n\t\t\tresp.FlagKey = flag.Key\n\t\t\tresp.SegmentKeys = segmentKeys\n\n\t\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"segment based matched\", zap.Int(\"rank\", int(rollout.Rank)), zap.Strings(\"segments\", segmentKeys))\n\t\t\treturn resp, nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// If we have exhausted all rollouts and we still don't have a match, return flag enabled value.\n\tresp.Reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_DEFAULT_EVALUATION_REASON\n\tresp.Enabled = flag.Enabled\n\tresp.FlagKey = flag.Key\n\n\ts.logger.Debug(\"default rollout matched\", zap.Bool(\"enabled\", flag.Enabled))\n\treturn resp, nil\n}\n\n// Batch takes in a list of *evaluation.EvaluationRequest and returns their respective responses.\nfunc (s *Server) Batch(ctx context.Context, b *rpcevaluation.BatchEvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.BatchEvaluationResponse, error) {\n\tresp := &rpcevaluation.BatchEvaluationResponse{\n\t\tResponses: make([]*rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponse, 0, len(b.Requests)),\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, req := range b.GetRequests() {\n\t\t// this is not ideal as it could lead to a lot of swapping the environment store if requests are coming in for different environments\n\t\t// we will need to document that while you CAN use different environments in the same request, it is not recommended and could have a performance impact\n\t\t// but since we are using an in-memory map it's probably not that bad\n\t\tenv, err := s.store.Get(ctx, req.EnvironmentKey)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t// try to get the environment from the context\n\t\t\t// this is for backwards compatibility with v1\n\t\t\tenv, err = s.store.GetFromContext(ctx)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tstore, err := env.EvaluationStore()\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tf, err := store.GetFlag(ctx, storage.NewResource(req.NamespaceKey, req.FlagKey, storage.WithReference(b.Reference)))\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tvar errnf errs.ErrNotFound\n\t\t\tif errors.As(err, &errnf) {\n\t\t\t\teresp := &rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponse{\n\t\t\t\t\tType: rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponseType_ERROR_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE,\n\t\t\t\t\tResponse: &rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponse_ErrorResponse{\n\t\t\t\t\t\tErrorResponse: &rpcevaluation.ErrorEvaluationResponse{\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tFlagKey:      req.FlagKey,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: req.NamespaceKey,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tReason:       rpcevaluation.ErrorEvaluationReason_NOT_FOUND_ERROR_EVALUATION_REASON,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tresp.Responses = append(resp.Responses, eresp)\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tswitch f.Type {\n\t\tcase core.FlagType_BOOLEAN_FLAG_TYPE:\n\t\t\tres, err := s.boolean(ctx, store, env, f, req)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif s.tracingEnabled {\n\t\t\t\ts.addEvaluationEvent(ctx, env, req.NamespaceKey, req.FlagKey, req.EntityId, req.RequestId,\n\t\t\t\t\ttracing.AttributeVariant.Bool(res.Enabled),\n\t\t\t\t\ttracing.AttributeReason.String(tracing.ReasonToValue(res.Reason)),\n\t\t\t\t\ttracing.AttributeSegments.StringSlice(res.SegmentKeys),\n\t\t\t\t\ttracing.AttributeFlagTypeBoolean,\n\t\t\t\t)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\teresp := &rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponse{\n\t\t\t\tType: rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponseType_BOOLEAN_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE,\n\t\t\t\tResponse: &rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponse_BooleanResponse{\n\t\t\t\t\tBooleanResponse: res,\n\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tresp.Responses = append(resp.Responses, eresp)\n\t\tcase core.FlagType_VARIANT_FLAG_TYPE:\n\t\t\tres, err := s.variant(ctx, store, env, f, req)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif s.tracingEnabled {\n\t\t\t\ts.addEvaluationEvent(ctx, env, req.NamespaceKey, req.FlagKey, req.EntityId, req.RequestId,\n\t\t\t\t\ttracing.AttributeMatch.Bool(res.Match),\n\t\t\t\t\ttracing.AttributeVariant.String(res.VariantKey),\n\t\t\t\t\ttracing.AttributeReason.String(tracing.ReasonToValue(res.Reason)),\n\t\t\t\t\ttracing.AttributeSegments.StringSlice(res.SegmentKeys),\n\t\t\t\t\ttracing.AttributeFlagTypeVariant,\n\t\t\t\t)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\teresp := &rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponse{\n\t\t\t\tType: rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponseType_VARIANT_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE,\n\t\t\t\tResponse: &rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponse_VariantResponse{\n\t\t\t\t\tVariantResponse: res,\n\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tresp.Responses = append(resp.Responses, eresp)\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\treturn nil, errs.ErrInvalidf(\"unknown flag type: %s\", f.Type)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn resp, nil\n}\n\n// matchConstraints is a utility function that will return if all or any constraints have matched for a segment depending\n// on the match type.\nfunc (s *Server) matchConstraints(evalCtx map[string]string, constraints []storage.EvaluationConstraint, segmentMatchType core.MatchType, entityId string) (bool, string, error) {\n\tconstraintMatches := 0\n\n\tvar reason string\n\n\tfor _, c := range constraints {\n\t\tv := evalCtx[c.Property]\n\n\t\tvar (\n\t\t\tmatch bool\n\t\t\terr   error\n\t\t)\n\n\t\tswitch c.Type {\n\t\tcase core.ComparisonType_STRING_COMPARISON_TYPE:\n\t\t\tmatch = matchesString(c, v)\n\t\tcase core.ComparisonType_NUMBER_COMPARISON_TYPE:\n\t\t\tmatch, err = matchesNumber(c, v)\n\t\tcase core.ComparisonType_BOOLEAN_COMPARISON_TYPE:\n\t\t\tmatch, err = matchesBool(c, v)\n\t\tcase core.ComparisonType_DATETIME_COMPARISON_TYPE:\n\t\t\tmatch, err = matchesDateTime(c, v)\n\t\tcase core.ComparisonType_ENTITY_ID_COMPARISON_TYPE:\n\t\t\tmatch = matchesString(c, entityId)\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\treturn false, reason, errs.ErrInvalid(\"unknown constraint type\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"error matching constraint\", zap.String(\"property\", c.Property), zap.Error(err))\n\t\t\t// don't return here because we want to continue to evaluate the other constraints\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif match {\n\t\t\t// increase the matchCount\n\t\t\tconstraintMatches++\n\n\t\t\tswitch segmentMatchType {\n\t\t\tcase core.MatchType_ANY_MATCH_TYPE:\n\t\t\t\t// can short circuit here since we had at least one match\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\t// keep looping as we need to match all constraints\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t// no match\n\t\t\tswitch segmentMatchType {\n\t\t\tcase core.MatchType_ALL_MATCH_TYPE:\n\t\t\t\t// we can short circuit because we must match all constraints\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\t// keep looping to see if we match the next constraint\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tmatched := true\n\n\tswitch segmentMatchType {\n\tcase core.MatchType_ALL_MATCH_TYPE:\n\t\tif len(constraints) != constraintMatches {\n\t\t\treason = \"did not match ALL constraints\"\n\t\t\tmatched = false\n\t\t}\n\n\tcase core.MatchType_ANY_MATCH_TYPE:\n\t\tif len(constraints) > 0 && constraintMatches == 0 {\n\t\t\treason = \"did not match ANY constraints\"\n\t\t\tmatched = false\n\t\t}\n\tdefault:\n\t\treason = fmt.Sprintf(\"unknown match type %d\", segmentMatchType)\n\t\tmatched = false\n\t}\n\n\treturn matched, reason, nil\n}\n\nfunc crc32Num(entityID string, salt string) uint {\n\treturn 100\n)\n\nfunc matchesString(c storage.EvaluationConstraint, v string) bool {\n\tswitch c.Operator {\n\tcase flipt.OpEmpty:\n\t\treturn len(strings.TrimSpace(v)) == 0\n\tcase value)\n\t}\n\n\treturn false\n}\n\nfunc matchesNumber(c storage.EvaluationConstraint, v string) (bool, error) {\n\tswitch c.Operator {\n\tcase flipt.OpNotPresent:\n\t\treturn segmentMatchType, nil\n\t} // end rule loop\n\n\treturn resp, \"\", nil\n}\n\n// matchConstraints is a utility function that will return if all or any constraints have matched for a segment depending\n// on the match type.\nfunc (e *Evaluator) matchConstraints(evalCtx map[string]string, constraints []storage.EvaluationConstraint, segmentMatchType flipt.MatchType, entityId string) (bool, string, error) {\n\tconstraintMatches := 0\n\n\tvar reason string\n\n\tfor _, c := range constraints {\n\t\tv := evalCtx[c.Property]\n\n\t\tvar (\n\t\t\tmatch bool\n\t\t\terr match all constraints\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\t// keep looping to see if we match the next constraint\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tvar matched = true\n\n\tswitch segmentMatchType {\n\tcase flipt.MatchType_ALL_MATCH_TYPE:\n\t\tif len(constraints) != constraintMatches {\n\t\t\treason = \"did not match ALL constraints\"\n\t\t\tmatched = false\n\t\t}\n\n\tcase flipt.MatchType_ANY_MATCH_TYPE:\n\t\tif len(constraints) > 0 && constraintMatches == 0 {\n\t\t\treason = \"did not match ANY constraints\"\n\t\t\tmatched = false\n\t\t}\n\tdefault:\n\t\treason = 100\n)\n\nfunc matchesString(c storage.EvaluationConstraint, v string) bool {\n\tswitch c.Operator {\n\tcase flipt.OpEmpty:\n\t\treturn len(strings.TrimSpace(v)) == 0\n\tcase flipt.OpNotEmpty:\n\t\treturn len(strings.TrimSpace(v)) != 0\n\t}\n\n\tif v == \"\" {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\n\tvalue := c.Value\n\n\tswitch c.Operator {\n\tcase flipt.OpEQ:\n\t\treturn value == false\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn slices.Contains(values, v)\n\tcase flipt.OpIsNotOneOf:\n\t\tvalues := []string{}\n\t\tif err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(value), &values); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn !slices.Contains(values, v)\n\t}\n\n\treturn false\n}\n\nfunc matchesNumber(c storage.EvaluationConstraint, v string) (bool, error) {\n\tswitch c.Operator {\n\tcase errs.ErrInvalidf(\"parsing number from %q\", c.Value)\n\t}\n\n\tswitch c.Operator {\n\tcase flipt.OpEQ:\n\t\treturn value == n, nil\n\tcase flipt.OpNEQ:\n\t\treturn value != n, nil\n\tcase }

enum EvaluationReason {
    UNKNOWN_EVALUATION_REASON = 0;
    FLAG_DISABLED_EVALUATION_REASON = 1;
    MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON = 2;
    DEFAULT_EVALUATION_REASON = 3;
}

  UNKNOWN_ERROR_EVALUATION_REASON = 0;
  NOT_FOUND_ERROR_EVALUATION_REASON = 1;
}

enum EvaluationResponseType {
  VARIANT_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE = 0;
  BOOLEAN_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE = 1;
  ERROR_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE = 2;
}

message EvaluationResponse {
    EvaluationResponseType type = 1;
    oneof response {
        BooleanEvaluationResponse boolean_response = 2;
        VariantEvaluationResponse variant_response = 3;
        ErrorEvaluationResponse error_response = 4;
    }
}

// addEvaluationEvent adds a tracing event for flag evaluation with the appropriate attributes
func (s *Server) addEvaluationEvent(ctx context.Context, env environments.Environment, namespaceKey, flagKey, entityID, requestID string, attrs ...attribute.KeyValue) {
	span := trace.SpanFromContext(ctx)
	baseAttrs := []attribute.KeyValue{
		tracing.AttributeEnvironment.String(env.Key()),
		tracing.AttributeNamespace.String(namespaceKey),
		tracing.AttributeFlag.String(flagKey),
	}

	if entityID != "" {
		baseAttrs = append(baseAttrs, tracing.AttributeEntityID.String(entityID))
	}
	if requestID != "" {
		baseAttrs = append(baseAttrs, tracing.AttributeRequestID.String(requestID))
	}

	baseAttrs = append(baseAttrs, attrs...)
	span.AddEvent(tracing.Event, trace.WithAttributes(baseAttrs...))
}

// Evaluate evaluates a flag for a given context and returns the evaluation response
// along with the segment match type (ANY/ALL) and any error that occurred.
func (e *Evaluator) Evaluate(ctx context.Context, flag *flipt.Flag, r *rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest) (resp *rpcevaluation.VariantEvaluationResponse, segmentMatchType string, err error) {
	resp = &rpcevaluation.VariantEvaluationResponse{
		FlagKey:   flag.Key,
		RequestId: r.RequestId,
	}

	// Check if flag is disabled
	if !flag.Enabled {
		resp.Match = false

# Flipt segment_match_type Field Implementation

## Overview
Successfully added a `segment_match_type` string field to the `VariantEvaluationResponse` message in Flipt's evaluation responses. This field indicates whether a segment matched using `"ALL"` (all constraints matched) or `"ANY"` (at least one constraint matched) logic.

## Files Modified

### 1. Protocol Buffer Definition
**File**: `rpc/flipt/evaluation/evaluation.proto`
- **Change**: Added `string segment_match_type = 10;` to the `VariantEvaluationResponse` message (line 76)
- **Field Number**: 10 (sequential after `flag_key = 9`)
- **Type**: String
- **Values**: `"ANY"`, `"ALL"`, or `""` (empty when no segment matched)

### 2. Generated Protocol Buffer Code
**File**: `rpc/flipt/evaluation/evaluation.pb.go`

#### Structure Field Added (line 833)
```go
SegmentMatchType      string                 `protobuf:"bytes,10,opt,name=segment_match_type,json=segmentMatchType,proto3"`
```

#### Getter Method Added (lines 931-937)
```go
func (x *VariantEvaluationResponse) GetSegmentMatchType() string {
    if x != nil {
        return x.SegmentMatchType
    }
    return ""
}
```

### 3. Server Implementation - Variant Evaluation
**File**: `internal/server/evaluation/evaluation.go`

#### Variable Declaration (line 180)
```go
var segmentMatchType string
```

#### Segment Operator Logic (lines 206-220)
```go
switch rule.SegmentOperator {
case core.SegmentOperator_OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR:
    if segmentMatches < 1 {
        s.logger.Debug("did not match ANY segments")
        continue
    }
    segmentMatchType = "ANY"
case core.SegmentOperator_AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR:
    if len(rule.Segments) != segmentMatches {
        s.logger.Debug("did not match ALL segments")
        continue
    }
    segmentMatchType = "ALL"
}
```

USAGE INSTRUCTIONS
================================================================================

The modified file /workspace/legacy_evaluator.go can be used as a drop-in
replacement for the original internal/server/evaluation/legacy_evaluator.go
in the Flipt project.

Note: This change modifies the public signature of the Evaluate method, so
all call sites must be updated to handle the new segmentMatchType return value.

Call sites should be updated from:
  resp, err := evaluator.Evaluate(ctx, flag, request)

To:
  resp, segmentMatchType, err := evaluator.Evaluate(ctx, flag, request)

The segmentMatchType will contain:
  - "ANY" when rule.SegmentOperator is OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR
  - "ALL" when rule.SegmentOperator is AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR
  - ""    for error cases or when no rule matches

# Flipt segment_match_type Field - Implementation Complete

## Executive Summary

Successfully implemented the `segment_match_type` field for Flipt's evaluation responses. This cross-language change includes protobuf schema modifications and Go server code updates.

### 2. Generated Protobuf Code

### 3. Evaluation Server Code

  - AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR → "ALL"

### 4. Legacy Evaluator
**Location**: `internal/server/evaluation/legacy_evaluator.go`
- **Signature Change** (line 38): Added segmentMatchType return value
- **Return Updates**: All 11+ return statements updated to include field

## Implementation Details

### Segment Match Type Values
- `"ANY"`: At least one segment matched (OR operator)
- `"ALL"`: All segments matched (AND operator)  
- `""`: No segment matched (empty case)

- Proto3 syntax
- Field number 10 (valid, no collision)
- Optional field with default empty string
- Proper JSON serialization (snake_case)
